  <script>
    var ytpreload = ytpreload || {};
    ytpreload.SnapClassList = ['content-snap-width-1', 'content-snap-width-2',
                               'content-snap-width-3'];
    ytpreload.getSnapClass = function(guidePinned) {
      var SCROLLBAR_WIDTH = 21;
      var CONTENT_PADDING = 50;
      var GUIDE_WIDTH = 230;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_2 = 1056;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_3 = 1262;
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;

      var spaceForContent = screenWidth - SCROLLBAR_WIDTH - CONTENT_PADDING;
      if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle() && guidePinned) {
        spaceForContent -= GUIDE_WIDTH;
      }

      if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_3) {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[2];
      } else if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_2){
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[1];
      } else {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[0];
      }

    };
    ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS = 'guide-pinned';
    ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS = 'show-guide';
    ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle = function() {
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;
      return screenWidth >= 1251;
    };
    (function() {
      var htmlEl = document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0];
      var classList = [htmlEl.className];
        if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle()) {
          classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS);
            classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS);
        }
        classList.push(' ', ytpreload.getSnapClass(
            true));
      htmlEl.className = classList.join(' ');
    })();
  </script>

     <h2 class="intro big">Military/Veterans</h2> 
     <img class="centerImg header" alt="" width="582" height="247" src="/Images/military_Veterans2.jpg" /> 
     <div class="grid_10 prefix_1 suffix_1 alpha omega"> 
      <div class="clearfix centerTxt"> 
       <h3 class="verd intro grey" style="margin-bottom: 0;">High-speed academic programs, assistance with<br /> educational benefits and strong support. </h3> 
       <a class="rightArrowCTA xlarge" href="/Content/PDFs/checklist_military_veteran.pdf">Print a Military/Veteran Checklist</a> 
      </div> 
      <hr class="style1" style="margin-bottom: 30px;" /> 
      <div class="genericBody version2 verd clearfix"> 
       <div class="grid_5 alpha"> 
        <h4>How to Get In </h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li><strong><a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Admissions/meetCounselor">Contact an admissions counselor</a>!</strong> Using your transcripts, they can determine if you should apply now or need additional course work, and whether you should apply as a <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Admissions/pathsAdmissions#incomingFreshman">freshman</a> or <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Admissions/pathsAdmissions#transferStudents">transfer</a>.</li> 
         <li>Use the <a href="http://admission.universityofcalifornia.edu/transfer/transfer-admission-planner/index.html">Transfer Admission Planner (TAP)</a> to plan and track your course work.</li> 
         <li><strong>Secure Your Future at UCR Now!</strong> <em>Guarantee</em> your admission with our <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/WhyUCR/ourGuarantee#transferStudents"> Transfer Admission Guarantee (TAG)</a>.</li> 
        </ul> 
        <h4>How to Apply</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Submit your application between November 1 and November 30. <strong>All applications are due November 30!</strong></li> 
         <li>Applications are only accepted in November <strong>for a start date the following fall.</strong> Students are not admitted mid-year. </li> 
         <li>See a <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Apply">step-by-step guide</a> to the application process. Gather information early and give yourself plenty of time before the deadline!</li> 
         <li><a href="/Content/PDFs/checklist_military_veteran.pdf">Print a Military/Veteran Checklist</a> for a detailed timeline.</li> 
        </ul> 
        <h4>How You Can Afford It</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li><a href="http://www.specialservices.ucr.edu/veterans/Pages/default.aspx">Student Special Services</a> will help you maximize your educational benefits.</li> 
         <li>See <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/PayingForCollege/costEstimator"> how affordable </a> UCR is and the <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/PayingForCollege/financialAidScholarships"> many ways </a>we make college possible.</li> 
         <li><a href="http://www.specialservices.ucr.edu/veterans/gIBill/Pages/default.aspx"> Learn about state and federal military/veteran educational benefits, including the Post-9/11 GI Bill&reg;.</a></li> 
         <li>Our <a href="http://operationeducation.ucr.edu/"> Operation Education Scholarship</a> provides extensive support and is open to those disabled on active duty after 9/11/01 (and their spouses). </li> 
         <li>Veterans are eligible for exemption from the <a href="http://www.sbs.ucr.edu/students/deferred_payment_plan.html">Deferred Payment Plan</a> application fee and the first late fee each quarter. </li> 
         <li>The majority of UCR students <a href="http://collegeportrait.ucr.edu/success_progress.html"> graduate in four years.</a></li> 
        </ul> 
        <h4>How You Will Fit In</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li><a href="https://www.facebook.com/groups/UCRstudentvets/">Connect with current UCR military/veteran students on Facebook.</a></li> 
         <li>Our <a href="http://well.ucr.edu/Peers/Pages/NetworkofPeers.aspx">Military/Veteran Peer Mentors</a> are happy to show you the ropes!</li> 
         <li>Meet <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/WhyUCR/ourStudents">our diverse students</a>.</li> 
         <li>Plug right in to <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/CampusLife">campus life</a>.</li> 
         <li>Live in our <a href="http://housing.ucr.edu/liveUCR/special-interest-housing.aspx">Transfer Student Theme Hall</a>, <a href="http://housing.ucr.edu/housing-options/campus-apartments/">campus apartments</a> or <a href="http://housing.ucr.edu/housing-options/family-student-housing.aspx">family housing</a>. Our Housing office can help you find a military roommate (if desired) and will work with you if your GI Bill payment is late.</li> 
         <li>Come to <a href="http://highlanderday.ucr.edu/">Highlander Day</a> and meet us in person.</li> 
        </ul> 
       </div> 
       <div class="grid_5 omega"> 
        <h4>How We Stand Out</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li>As an acclaimed research university, our <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Academics/collegesSchoolsMajors"> academic programs</a> are UC solid. From business and engineering to science and humanities, you will graduate with a degree the world respects.</li> 
         <li>We are a <a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/6766">GI Jobs Magazine Military Friendly School,</a> an honor given to the top fifteen percent of schools doing the most for their military/veteran students. </li> 
         <li>At UCR, you can <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/WhyUCR/ourResearch">conduct research as an undergraduate.</a></li> 
         <li><a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/WhyUCR/ourRankings">See how we rank</a> as a UC rising star.</li> 
         <li>See <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/WhyUCR">50 more good reasons</a> to choose UCR.</li> 
        </ul> 
        <h4>How We Support You</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li> <a href="http://www.specialservices.ucr.edu/Pages/default.aspx">Student Special Services</a> will assist you with everything from processing benefits to setting you up with disability accommodations for which you may qualify.</li> 
         <li><a href="/Content/PDFs/veterans_support_team_brochure.pdf">Our Veterans Support Team</a> provides points of contact campus-wide.</li> 
         <li><a href="http://well.ucr.edu/Peers/Pages/NetworkofPeers.aspx"> Military/Veteran Peer Mentors</a> help you transition to student life, connect you to the campus community and can be a friend when you need one.</li> 
         <li> UCR's <a href="http://highlanderlink.ucr.edu/organization/avs">Association of Veterans and Service Members</a> offers advocacy, workshops, scholarships, policy news and more. </li> 
         <li>Enjoy priority registration (continuing students), special veteran family events, leaves of absence when deployed and our new veterans' lounge.</li> 
         <li>Discover our <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/students/ethnic_gender.html"> Ethnic &amp; Gender Programs.</a></li> 
         <li> Learn about free tutoring at the <a href="http://arc.ucr.edu/"> Academic Resource Center.</a></li> 
         <li>Explore <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Academics/honorsPrograms"> honors opportunities.</a></li> 
        </ul> 
        <h4>How to Stay Connected</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Like us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/ucradmissions" target="_blank">Facebook</a>.</li> 
         <li>Follow us on <a href="https://twitter.com/ucradmissions" target="_blank">Twitter</a>.</li> 
         <li>Follow us on <a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/" target="_blank">Tumblr</a>.</li> 
         <li> Join UCR Student Veterans and Service Members on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/groups/UCRstudentvets/"> Facebook</a>.</li> 
         <li>Like UCR Veterans Services (Student Special Services) on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/UCRVets">Facebook</a>.</li> 
         <li>Follow UCR Veterans Services (Student Special Services) on <a href="https://twitter.com/UCRVets">Twitter</a>.</li> 
        </ul> 
        <h4>How to Get Help</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li><a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Admissions/meetCounselor">Contact an admissions counselor</a>.</li> 
         <li>Benefits questions?<a href="http://www.specialservices.ucr.edu/contact/Pages/default.aspx"> Contact Student Special Services.</a> </li> 
         <li>See answers to <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Home/FAQ">frequently asked questions.</a></li> 
        </ul> 
       </div> 
      </div>

                Y.Global.on('saveforlater|saveforlater:newsaved', function()
                {
                    var tabIcon = Y.one('#yucsHead .yucs-avatar.yucs-menu_anchor'),
                        sflIcon = tabIcon && tabIcon.one('.sfl-icon');

                    if (tabIcon && !sflIcon)
                    {
                        var repeats = 0, callback = null;
                        
                        sflIcon = Y.Node.create('<i class="icon-y-xsmall selected sfl-icon"></i>');
                        sflIcon.setStyles({
                            'opacity': 0,
                            'boxShadow': '0px 0px 20px #400090'
                        });
                        tabIcon.prepend(sflIcon);

                        callback = function ()
                        {
                            sflIcon.transition({
                                duration: 0.6,
                                opacity: (repeats + 1) % 2
                            });
                            repeats++;
                            if (repeats < 4)
                                Y.later(600, this, callback); // the animation duration for each is 600ms
                            else
                                Y.later(600, this, function () {sflIcon.remove();});
                        };
                        Y.later(10, this, callback);
                    }
                });});

                    DARLA_CONFIG.onFinishParse = function(eventId, result) {
                        var noads = [], ps = result.ps(),
                            i, l, position, posObj, mutexPos, posName, container, display,
                            re = /([A-Z0-9]+)(-[0-9]+)*/;
                    
                        for (i = 0, l = ps.length; i < l; i++) {
                            position = ps[i];
                            posObj = result.item(position);
                            if (!posObj || posObj.hasErr) {
                                noads.push(position);
                            }
                        }

                        // handle mutual exclusion for client side fetched ads
                        if (eventId === LB_EVENT || eventId === AUTO_EVENT) {
                            for (position in MUTEX_ADS) {
                                if (MUTEX_ADS.hasOwnProperty(position) && ps.indexOf(position) >= 0 && noads.indexOf(position) === -1) {
                                    for (i = 0, l = MUTEX_ADS[position].length; i < l; i++) {
                                        mutexPos = MUTEX_ADS[position][i];
                                        if (ps.indexOf(mutexPos) >= 0 && noads.indexOf(mutexPos) === -1) {
                                            noads.push(mutexPos);
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            for (i = 0, l = ps.length; i < l; i++) {
                                position = ps[i];
                                posName = re.exec(position)[1];
                                container = Y.one('.yom-ad-'+posName);
                                if (container) {
                                    display = container.getStyle('display');
                                    if (display === 'none' && noads.indexOf(position) === -1) {
                                        container.show();
                                    } else if (display !== 'none' && noads.indexOf(position) >= 0) {
                                        container.hide();
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    
                        // reset the hight of the LDRB container
                        if (ps.indexOf('LDRB') >= 0 && result.item('LDRB')) {
                            
                            if (noads.indexOf('LDRB') <= 0){
                                var clearAdModule = Y.one('#yom-ad-LDRB');
                                if (result.item('LDRB').size + '' !== '1x1') {
                                    clearAdModule.setStyle('height', '');
                                    Y.log('LDRB height is reset to blank.', 'info', 'darla');
                                } else {
                                    clearAdModule.setStyle('height', '5px');
                                    Y.log('LDRB height is reset to 5px.', 'info', 'darla');
                                }
                            } else {
                                Y.log('LDRB is noad or size is 1x1', 'info', 'darla');
                            }
                        }                    
                    }                    /* preparing the Nodes with iframes. Note this would be hidden iframe and not visible in the DOM */

                        return {
                            _prepareNodes: function() {
                                for(var cleanId in nodes){
                                    var center = Y.one("#"+cleanId+" > center");
                                    if(center != null && center && !Y.one("#" + nodes[cleanId].id)){
                                        center.set("innerHTML","");
                                        center.insert(nodes[cleanId].node);
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        };
                    })();

                    /* setting up DARLA events */
                    var w = window,
                        D = w.DARLA,
                        C = w.DARLA_CONFIG,
                        DM = w.DOC_DOMAIN_SET || 0;
                    if (D) {
                        if (D && C) {
                            C.dm = DM;
                        }
                        
                        DARLA_CONFIG.nodeMgr._prepareNodes();
                        
                        /* setting DARLA configuration */
                        DARLA.config(C);

                        /* prefetch Ads if applicable */
                        DARLA.prefetched("fc");

                        /* rendering prefetched Ad */
                        DARLA.render();  
                    }

                    return {
                        event: function (eventId, spaceId, adsSa) {
                            if (window.DARLA && eventId) {
                                DARLA_CONFIG.nodeMgr._prepareNodes();
                                var eventConfig = {};
                                if (!isNaN(spaceId)) {
                                    eventConfig.sp = spaceId;
                                }
                                /* Site attributes */
                                adsSa = (typeof adsSa !== "undefined" && adsSa !== null) ? adsSa : "";
                                eventConfig.sa = DARLA_CONFIG.events[eventId].sa_orig.replace ? DARLA_CONFIG.events[eventId].sa_orig.replace("ADSSA", adsSa) : "";
                                DARLA.event(eventId, eventConfig);
                            }
                        },
                        render: function() {
                            if (!!(Y.one('#yom-slideshow-lightbox') || Y.one('#content-lightbox') || false)) {
                                /* skip configuring DARLA in case of lightbox being triggered */
                            } else {
                                // abort current darla action
                                if (DARLA && DARLA.abort) {
                                    DARLA.abort();
                                }

                                /* prepare node is mainly for injected ad, eg. LREC within story body */
                                DARLA_CONFIG.nodeMgr._prepareNodes();

                                /* setting DARLA configuration */
                                DARLA.config(DARLA_CONFIG);

                                /* prefetch Ads if applicable */
                                DARLA.prefetched("fc");

                                /* rendering prefetched Ad */
                                DARLA.render();  
                            }
                        }
                    };

                })(); /* End of YUI.AdsDarla */

                    YUI.AdsDarla.darla = { fetch: (Y.bind(YUI.AdsDarla.event, YUI.AdsDarla, 'darla')) };                YUI.AdsDarla.fetch = YUI.AdsDarla.darla.fetch;
                Y.Global.fire('darla:ready');

     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <h1 class="page-header">Academic Affairs</h1> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row-fluid"> 
      <div class="span4 hero-unit"> 
       <p>We are a systemwide resource for academic excellence in research, teaching and public service.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p>The Office of the Provost builds on the energy and academic strength of UCs campuses to enhance the systems educational impact. We help recruit and retain outstanding professors and provide them with the support they need to succeed. We promote excellence through programs that help prepare, recruit and support undergraduate, graduate and professional students. We manage programs that help position UC and California as engines of economic, social and cultural development. And we ensure that UC remains on the cutting edge of innovation in teaching and learning by supporting new academic initiatives.</p>
      </div> 
      <div class="span4"> 
       <div class="row-fluid dotted-bottom"> 
        <div class="span4 dept-head"> 
         <img alt="Aim&eacute;e Dorr" src="_images/shot_47_adorr_040.jpg" />
        </div> 
        <div class="span8"> 
         <p class="blue"> <a href="http://universityofcalifornia.edu/news/aimee-dorr-serve-provost-uc-system">Aim&eacute;e Dorr</a> </p> 
         <p>Provost and Executive Vice President</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon staff" href="immediate-office-staff/index.html">Staff Directory</a>
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row-fluid blustripe dept-unit"> 
      <h2 class="nobtm">DEPARTMENTS/DIVISIONS</h2> 
      <div class="row-fluid col5"> 
       <div class="span3"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/academic-personnel/index.html">Academic Personnel</a> </h3> 
        <p>Coordinates policies and programs regarding faculty recruitment, diversity, retention, academic freedom, responsibilities and advancement.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/academic-personnel/academic-personnel-policy/index.html">Academic Personnel Manual</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/academic-personnel/compensation/index.html">Compensation</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/ucadvance/index.html">UC ADVANCE PAID Program</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/academic-personnel/data-and-analysis/index.html">Faculty diversity reports &amp; analyses</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span3"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/academic-planning-programs-coordination/index.html">Academic Programs and Coordination</a> </h3> 
        <p>Evaluates and plans for student enrollment, degree achievement and systemwide academic program development and manages systemwide academic and publishing programs.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/academic-planning-programs-coordination/academic-planning/accreditation.html">Accreditation resources</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/uconline/index.html">UC Online</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/academic-planning-programs-coordination/programs-and-initiatives/publishing/index.html">Publishing initiatives</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span3"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="http://ucanr.edu/">Agriculture and Natural Resources</a> </h3> 
        <p>Serves as the bridge between local issues and the power of UC research to bring practical, science-based answers to Californians.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="http://ucanr.edu/Publications_524/">ANR publications</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="http://ucanr.edu/ANR_Offices/">ANR offices</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="http://ucanr.edu/4-H/">4-H Youth Development</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span3"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/education-partnerships/index.html">Education Partnerships</a> </h3> 
        <p>Manages and evaluates student and teacher preparation programs and works with the CCC and CSU systems to enhance the accessibility of university degrees.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/education-partnerships/programs/index.html">College access programs</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/education-partnerships/programs/statewide-partnerships/index.html">Statewide partnerships</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/education-partnerships/reports-and-statistics/reports-and-accountability/index.html">Reports and accountability</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/education-partnerships/reports-and-statistics/index.html">Program outcomes</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row-fluid dept-unit"> 
      <div class="row-fluid col5"> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/institutional-research/index.html">Institutional Research and Academic Planning</a> </h3> 
        <p>Provides information and analysis in support of university management, planning and decision-making.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/institutional-research/data-reports/uc-data/index.html">UC data and key reports</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/institutional-research/resources/index.html">Campus data resources</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/institutional-research/_files/2011-uc-time-doctorate.pdf">Time-to-doctorate at UC (pdf)</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/research-graduate-studies/index.html">Research and Graduate Studies</a> </h3> 
        <p>Coordinates systemwide policies for technology transfer, intellectual property and graduate study and manages a portfolio of grants.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/research-grants-program/index.html">Research Grants Program Office</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="http://ucop.edu/research/nrs/">Natural Reserve System</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/innovation-alliances-services/index.html">Innovation Alliances and Services</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/graduate-studies/index.html">Graduate Studies</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/research-policy-analysis-coordination/index.html">Research Policy Analysis and Coordination</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/student-affairs/index.html">Student Affairs</a> </h3> 
        <p>Maintains UC's admissions process and portal, oversees student financial aid policies throughout the system and works closely with community colleges and high schools on courses and criteria for admission to UC.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/student-affairs/policies/index.html">Financial aid policies</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/student-affairs/data-and-reporting/index.html">Data and reporting</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/student-affairs/programs-and-initiatives/index.html">Student services programs</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row less3 novrflw"> 
      <div class="span4 grybx"> 
       <h4>Contact Us</h4> 
       <p> <br /> Academic Affairs<br /> University of California<br /> Office of the President<br /> 1111 Franklin St., 12th Floor<br /> Oakland, CA 94607<br /> </p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4 grybx"> 
       <h4>Innovative Learning Technology Initiative (ILTI)</h4> 
       <div class="flt-left">
        <a href="#"><img alt="${image.getChild('title').value}" src="_images/student-laptop.jpg" /></a>
       </div> 
       <p><span><span>ILTI aims to expand the use of innovative and high-quality online instruction to improve student access to high-demand courses.</span></span></p> 
       <p><a href="innovative-learning-technology-initiative/index.html">Learn more</a></p> 
      </div>

  <div class="pagewrapper"> 
   <h3 class="accessibility">Footer</h3> 
   <div id="colophon">
     The University of California, Riverside (
    <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR's enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus opened a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. A broadcast studio with fiber cable to the AT&amp;T Hollywood hub is available for live or taped interviews. UCR also has ISDN for radio interviews. To learn more, call (951) UCR-NEWS. 
   </div>
